I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
[feature] Add STS AssumeRole (cross-account IAM) support for Kafka async consumer
**Is your feature request related to a problem? Please describe.**

Currently, Centrifugo's Kafka async consumer supports AWS MSK IAM ("aws-msk-iam" SASL mechanism) by configuring AccessKey/SecretKey via the SASL user/password fields. However, it is missing support for using [AWS STS AssumeRole](https://docs.aws.amazon.com/STS/latest/APIReference/API_AssumeRole.html) for IAM authentication. This is needed to easily and securely connect to MSK clusters hosted in *other* AWS accounts, or when following best practices that require only temporary credentials.

Many organizations use cross-account setups (for instance, running Centrifugo in one AWS account and hosting MSK in another) and would prefer to use role assumption instead of sharing or rotating long-term IAM keys. This would also make it consistent with the SQS consumer, which already supports an `assume_role_arn` config field for cross-account access.

**Describe the solution you'd like.**

- Add `assume_role_arn` (or similar) and, optionally, `credentials_profile` options to the Kafka consumer config, matching the SQS consumer configuration style.
- At runtime, if the option is set, Centrifugo should use AWS STS (via the SDK) to obtain temporary credentials and use those for SASL authentication.
- The configuration should continue to support direct key input for backwards compatibility, but if both are set, `assume_role_arn` should take precedence.
- Document this option in the Kafka consumer section of the docs, including an example cross-account scenario.

**Who will benefit from this feature?**

- Teams needing to securely connect Centrifugo to MSK in other AWS accounts
- Users following AWS best practices (no long-lived IAM users/keys)
- Environments requiring tighter IAM and audit controls

**Additional context**
- SQS consumer already supports assume role via `assume_role_arn`. Parity in Kafka consumer would be very useful.
- This feature would use the AWS Go SDK's `stscreds` provider under the hood, as with SQS.

</pr_description>

    30	        topicPartitionBeforePauseCh    chan topicPartition
    31	        topicPartitionPauseProceedCh   chan struct{}
    32	        fetchTopicPartitionSubmittedCh chan kgo.FetchTopicPartition
    33	        // leaveGroupOnShutdown when true sends a manual LeaveGroup request on shutdown.
    34	        // Used only in tests to simulate the old behavior with dynamic instance IDs.
    35	        leaveGroupOnShutdown bool
    36	}

    38	type topicPartition struct {
    39	        topic     string
    40	        partition int32
    41	}
    42	
    43	type KafkaConsumer struct {
    44	        name       string
    45	        client     *kgo.Client
    46	        dispatcher Dispatcher
    47	        config     KafkaConfig
    48	        // consumersMu protects the consumers map. During normal operation, concurrent access is already
    49	        // prevented: franz-go serializes assigned/revoked/lost callbacks, and BlockRebalanceOnPoll
    50	        // prevents callbacks from firing while pollUntilFatal reads the map. The mutex is needed
    51	        // for shutdown, when the main goroutine accesses the map (via allTopicPartitions/killConsumers)
    52	        // while the group management goroutine may still be running callbacks. Must not be held
    53	        // during killConsumers' wg.Wait() to avoid blocking concurrent callbacks.
    54	        consumersMu    sync.Mutex
    55	        consumers      map[topicPartition]*partitionConsumer
    56	        doneCh         chan struct{}
    57	        common         *consumerCommon
    58	        testOnlyConfig testOnlyConfig
    59	}
    60	
    61	func NewKafkaConsumer(
    62	        config KafkaConfig, dispatcher Dispatcher, common *consumerCommon,
    63	) (*KafkaConsumer, error) {
    64	        if len(config.Brokers) == 0 {
    65	                return nil, errors.New("brokers required")
    66	        }
    67	        if len(config.Topics) == 0 {
    68	                return nil, errors.New("topics required")
    69	        }
    70	        if len(config.ConsumerGroup) == 0 {
    71	                return nil, errors.New("consumer_group required")
    72	        }
    73	        if config.MaxPollRecords == 0 {
    74	                config.MaxPollRecords = 100
    75	        }
    76	        if config.FetchMaxWait == 0 {
    77	                config.FetchMaxWait = configtypes.Duration(500 * time.Millisecond)
    78	        }
    79	        if config.PartitionQueueMaxSize == -1 {
    80	                config.PartitionQueueMaxSize = 0
    81	        } else if config.PartitionQueueMaxSize == 0 {
    82	                config.PartitionQueueMaxSize = 1000
    83	        }
    84	        consumer := &KafkaConsumer{
    85	                name:       common.name,
    86	                dispatcher: dispatcher,
    87	                config:     config,
    88	                consumers:  make(map[topicPartition]*partitionConsumer),
    89	                doneCh:     make(chan struct{}),
    90	                common:     common,
    91	        }
    92	        cl, err := consumer.initClient()
    93	        if err != nil {
    94	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("error init Kafka client: %w", err)
    95	        }
    96	        consumer.client = cl
    97	        return consumer, nil
    98	}

   100	const kafkaClientID = "centrifugo"
   101	
   102	// kgoZerologAdapter adapts zerolog.Logger to kgo.Logger interface.
   103	type kgoZerologAdapter struct {
   104	        log zerolog.Logger
   105	}
   106	
   107	func (l *kgoZerologAdapter) Level() kgo.LogLevel {
   108	        switch {
   109	        case logging.Enabled(logging.TraceLevel):
   110	                return kgo.LogLevelDebug // Kafka client debug level is more like our trace.
   111	        case logging.Enabled(logging.InfoLevel):
   112	                return kgo.LogLevelInfo
   113	        case logging.Enabled(logging.WarnLevel):
   114	                return kgo.LogLevelWarn
   115	        case logging.Enabled(logging.ErrorLevel):
   116	                return kgo.LogLevelError
   117	        default:
   118	                return kgo.LogLevelNone
   119	        }
   120	}
   121	
   122	func (l *kgoZerologAdapter) Log(level kgo.LogLevel, msg string, keyvals ...any) {
   123	        var e *zerolog.Event
   124	        switch level {
   125	        case kgo.LogLevelError:
   126	                e = l.log.Error()
   127	        case kgo.LogLevelWarn:
   128	                e = l.log.Warn()
   129	        case kgo.LogLevelInfo:
   130	                e = l.log.Info()
   131	        case kgo.LogLevelDebug:
   132	                e = l.log.Trace() // Kafka client debug level is more like our trace.
   133	        default:
   134	                return
   135	        }
   136	        for i := 0; i+1 < len(keyvals); i += 2 {
   137	                if key, ok := keyvals[i].(string); ok {
   138	                        e = e.Interface(key, keyvals[i+1])
   139	                }
   140	        }
   141	        e.Msg(msg)
   142	}
   143	
   144	// leaveGroup sends a manual LeaveGroup request for static members. franz-go's Close does not
   145	// send LeaveGroup for static members by design. This method is only used in tests to simulate
   146	// the old behavior where dynamic instance IDs were combined with a manual LeaveGroup.
   147	func (c *KafkaConsumer) leaveGroup(ctx context.Context, client *kgo.Client) error {
   148	        req := kmsg.NewPtrLeaveGroupRequest()
   149	        req.Group = c.config.ConsumerGroup
   150	        instanceID := c.config.InstanceID
   151	        reason := "shutdown"
   152	        req.Members = []kmsg.LeaveGroupRequestMember{
   153	                {
   154	                        InstanceID: &instanceID,
   155	                        Reason:     &reason,
   156	                },
   157	        }
   158	        _, err := req.RequestWith(ctx, client)
   159	        return err
   160	}
   161	
   162	func (c *KafkaConsumer) initClient() (*kgo.Client, error) {
   163	        opts := []kgo.Opt{
   164	                kgo.SeedBrokers(c.config.Brokers...),
   165	                kgo.ConsumeTopics(c.config.Topics...),
   166	                kgo.ConsumerGroup(c.config.ConsumerGroup),
   167	                kgo.OnPartitionsAssigned(c.assigned),
   168	                kgo.OnPartitionsRevoked(c.revoked),
   169	                kgo.OnPartitionsLost(c.lost),
   170	                kgo.AutoCommitMarks(),
   171	                kgo.BlockRebalanceOnPoll(),
   172	                kgo.ClientID(kafkaClientID),
   173	                kgo.FetchMaxWait(time.Duration(c.config.FetchMaxWait)),
   174	                kgo.WithLogger(&kgoZerologAdapter{log: c.common.log}),
   175	        }
   176	        if c.config.InstanceID != "" { // Important to keep separate, otherwise pointer to empty string is used in kgo.InstanceID.
   177	                opts = append(opts, kgo.InstanceID(c.config.InstanceID))
   178	        }
   179	        if c.config.FetchMaxBytes > 0 {
   180	                opts = append(opts, kgo.FetchMaxBytes(c.config.FetchMaxBytes))
   181	        }
   182	        if !c.config.FetchReadUncommitted {
   183	                opts = append(opts, kgo.FetchIsolationLevel(kgo.ReadCommitted()))
   184	        } else {
   185	                opts = append(opts, kgo.FetchIsolationLevel(kgo.ReadUncommitted()))
   186	        }
   187	        if c.config.TLS.Enabled {
   188	                tlsConfig, err := c.config.TLS.ToGoTLSConfig("kafka:" + c.name)
   189	                if err != nil {
   190	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("error making TLS configuration: %w", err)
   191	                }
   192	                dialer := &tls.Dialer{
   193	                        NetDialer: &net.Dialer{Timeout: 10 * time.Second},
   194	                        Config:    tlsConfig,
   195	                }
   196	                opts = append(opts, kgo.Dialer(dialer.DialContext))
   197	        }
   198	
   199	        if c.config.SASLMechanism != "" {
   200	                switch c.config.SASLMechanism {
   201	                case "plain":
   202	                        opts = append(opts, kgo.SASL(plain.Auth{
   203	                                User: c.config.SASLUser,
   204	                                Pass: c.config.SASLPassword,
   205	                        }.AsMechanism()))
   206	                case "scram-sha-256":
   207	                        opts = append(opts, kgo.SASL(scram.Auth{
   208	                                User: c.config.SASLUser,
   209	                                Pass: c.config.SASLPassword,
   210	                        }.AsSha256Mechanism()))
   211	                case "scram-sha-512":
   212	                        opts = append(opts, kgo.SASL(scram.Auth{
   213	                                User: c.config.SASLUser,
   214	                                Pass: c.config.SASLPassword,
   215	                        }.AsSha512Mechanism()))
   216	                case "aws-msk-iam":
   217	                        opts = append(opts, kgo.SASL(aws.Auth{
   218	                                AccessKey: c.config.SASLUser,
   219	                                SecretKey: c.config.SASLPassword,
   220	                        }.AsManagedStreamingIAMMechanism()))
   221	                default:
   222	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("unsupported SASL mechanism: %s", c.config.SASLMechanism)
   223	                }
   224	        }
   225	
   226	        client, err := kgo.NewClient(opts...)
   227	        if err != nil {
   228	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("error initializing client: %w", err)
   229	        }
   230	        ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 5*time.Second)
   231	        defer cancel()
   232	        if err := client.Ping(ctx); err != nil {
   233	                client.Close()
   234	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("error ping Kafka: %w", err)
   235	        }
   236	        return client, nil
   237	}
   238	
   239	func (c *KafkaConsumer) Run(ctx context.Context) error {
   240	        defer func() {
   241	                close(c.doneCh)
   242	                if c.client != nil {
   243	                        // Stop all partition consumers first to ensure all offsets are marked.
   244	                        c.killConsumers(c.allTopicPartitions())
   245	                        if c.testOnlyConfig.leaveGroupOnShutdown && c.config.InstanceID != "" {
   246	                                // Test-only path simulating old behavior with dynamic instance IDs.
   247	                                // Commit before manual LeaveGroup — the coordinator rejects commits
   248	                                // from members that already left the group.
   249	                                closeCtx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 10*time.Second)
   250	                                defer cancel()
   251	                                if err := c.client.CommitMarkedOffsets(closeCtx); err != nil {
   252	                                        c.common.log.Error().Err(err).Msg("error committing marked offsets on shutdown")
   253	                                }
   254	                                if err := c.leaveGroup(closeCtx, c.client); err != nil {
   255	                                        c.common.log.Error().Err(err).Msg("error leaving consumer group")
   256	                                }
   257	                        }
   258	                        // CloseAllowingRebalance calls AllowRebalance (required since we use
   259	                        // BlockRebalanceOnPoll) and then Close. Close triggers the manage loop
   260	                        // exit which calls onRevoked with a valid client context and no

    28	type AwsSqsConsumerConfig = configtypes.AwsSqsConsumerConfig
    29	
    30	// AwsSqsConsumer consumes messages from AWS SQS (or SNS delivered to SQS).
    31	// It uses per-group ordering when enabled and supports both command and publication data modes.
    32	type AwsSqsConsumer struct {
    33	        config     AwsSqsConsumerConfig
    34	        dispatcher Dispatcher
    35	        client     *sqs.Client
    36	        common     *consumerCommon
    37	}
    38	
    39	type overrideEndpointResolver struct {
    40	        Endpoint endpoints.Endpoint
    41	}
    42	
    43	func (o overrideEndpointResolver) ResolveEndpoint(_ context.Context, _ sqs.EndpointParameters) (endpoints.Endpoint, error) {
    44	        return o.Endpoint, nil
    45	}
    46	
    47	// NewAwsSqsConsumer creates and initializes a new AwsSqsConsumer.
    48	func NewAwsSqsConsumer(
    49	        cfg AwsSqsConsumerConfig, dispatcher Dispatcher, common *consumerCommon,
    50	) (*AwsSqsConsumer, error) {
    51	        if err := cfg.Validate(); err != nil {
    52	                return nil, err
    53	        }
    54	
    55	        loadOpts := []func(*config.LoadOptions) error{
    56	                config.WithRegion(cfg.Region),
    57	        }
    58	        if cfg.CredentialsProfile != "" {
    59	                loadOpts = append(loadOpts, config.WithSharedConfigProfile(cfg.CredentialsProfile))
    60	        }
    61	
    62	        ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 5*time.Second)
    63	        defer cancel()
    64	        awsCfg, err := config.LoadDefaultConfig(ctx, loadOpts...)
    65	        if err != nil {
    66	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to load AWS config: %w", err)
    67	        }
    68	
    69	        var sqsOpts []func(*sqs.Options)
    70	        var client *sqs.Client
    71	        if cfg.LocalStackEndpoint != "" {
    72	                parsedURL, err := url.Parse(cfg.LocalStackEndpoint)
    73	                if err != nil {
    74	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to parse LocalStack endpoint: %w", err)
    75	                }
    76	                sqsOpts = append(sqsOpts,
    77	                        sqs.WithEndpointResolverV2(overrideEndpointResolver{
    78	                                Endpoint: endpoints.Endpoint{
    79	                                        URI: *parsedURL,
    80	                                },
    81	                        }),
    82	                )
    83	        }
    84	
    85	        // If AssumeRoleARN is provided, assume that role.
    86	        if cfg.AssumeRoleARN != "" {
    87	                stsClient := sts.NewFromConfig(awsCfg)
    88	                assumeRoleProvider := stscreds.NewAssumeRoleProvider(stsClient, cfg.AssumeRoleARN)
    89	                awsCfg.Credentials = aws.NewCredentialsCache(assumeRoleProvider)
    90	        }
    91	
    92	        client = sqs.NewFromConfig(awsCfg, sqsOpts...)
    93	
    94	        consumer := &AwsSqsConsumer{
    95	                config:     cfg,
    96	                dispatcher: dispatcher,
    97	                client:     client,
    98	                common:     common,
    99	        }
   100	        return consumer, nil
   101	}
   102	
   103	// Run is the main loop that receives messages from each queue and processes them in batches.
   104	func (c *AwsSqsConsumer) Run(ctx context.Context) error {
   105	        var wg sync.WaitGroup
   106	
   107	        maxConcurrency := c.config.MaxConcurrency
   108	        if maxConcurrency < 1 {
   109	                maxConcurrency = 1
   110	        }
   111	
   112	        // Spawn one goroutine per queue URL.
   113	        for _, queueURL := range c.config.Queues {
   114	                wg.Add(1)
   115	                go func(qURL string) {
   116	                        defer wg.Done()
   117	                        for {
   118	                                select {
   119	                                case <-ctx.Done():
   120	                                        return

   127	                                }

   130	                                if visibilityTimeoutSeconds < 1 {

   797	        // If not set the default 50MB is used.
   798	        FetchMaxBytes int32 `mapstructure:"fetch_max_bytes" json:"fetch_max_bytes" envconfig:"fetch_max_bytes" yaml:"fetch_max_bytes" toml:"fetch_max_bytes"`

   802	        // FetchReadUncommitted is a flag to enable reading uncommitted messages from Kafka. By default, this is false and Centrifugo uses ReadCommitted mode.
   803	        FetchReadUncommitted bool `mapstructure:"fetch_read_uncommitted" json:"fetch_read_uncommitted" envconfig:"fetch_read_uncommitted" default:"false" yaml:"fetch_read_uncommitted" toml:"fetch_read_uncommitted"`

   805	        // The actual queue size may exceed this value on `max_poll_records`, so this acts more like a threshold.
   806	        // If -1, pausing is done on every poll. If set, pausing only happens when queue size exceeds this threshold.

   835	                return errors.New("no Kafka brokers provided")
   836	        }
   837	        if len(c.Topics) == 0 {

   844	                return errors.New("no Kafka channels_header_name provided for publication data mode")
   845	        }
   846	        return nil
   847	}

    69	// This is a shortcut for using the ManagedStreamingIAM function and is useful

    79	// ManagedStreamingIAM returns a sasl mechanism that will call authFn whenever

    81	// session.
    82	func ManagedStreamingIAM(authFn func(context.Context) (Auth, error)) sasl.Mechanism {
    83	        return mskiam(authFn)

    88	func (fn mskiam) Authenticate(ctx context.Context, host string) (sasl.Session, []byte, error) {
    89	        auth, err := fn(ctx)
    90	        if err != nil {
    91	                return nil, nil, err
    92	        }
    93	
    94	        challenge, err := challenge(auth, host)
    95	        if err != nil {
    96	                return nil, nil, err
    97	        }
    98	
    99	        return new(session), challenge, nil
   100	}

   103	
   104	func (session) Challenge(resp []byte) (bool, []byte, error) {
   105	        if len(resp) == 0 {
   106	                return false, nil, errors.New("empty challenge response: failed")
   107	        }
   108	        return true, nil, nil
   109	}

   111	const service = "kafka-cluster"

   113	func challenge(auth Auth, host string) ([]byte, error) {
   114	        host, _, err := net.SplitHostPort(host) // we do not need the port
   115	        if err != nil {
   116	                return nil, err
   117	        }
   118	        region, err := identifyRegion(host)
   119	        if err != nil {
   120	                return nil, err
   121	        }
   122	
   123	        var (
   124	                timestamp = time.Now().UTC().Format("20060102T150405Z")
   125	                date      = timestamp[:8] // 20060102
   126	                scope     = scope(date, region)
   127	                v         = make(url.Values)
   128	        )
   129	
   130	        v.Set("Action", service+":Connect")
   131	        v.Set("X-Amz-Algorithm", "AWS4-HMAC-SHA256")
   132	        v.Set("X-Amz-Credential", auth.AccessKey+"/"+scope)
   133	        v.Set("X-Amz-Date", timestamp)
   134	        v.Set("X-Amz-Expires", "300") // 5 min
   135	        v.Set("X-Amz-SignedHeaders", "host")
   136	        if auth.SessionToken != "" {
   137	                v.Set("X-Amz-Security-Token", auth.SessionToken)
   138	        }
   139	
   140	        qps := strings.ReplaceAll(v.Encode(), "+", "%20")
   141	
   142	        canonicalRequest := task1(host, qps)
   143	        sts := task2(timestamp, scope, canonicalRequest)
   144	        signature := task3(auth.SecretKey, region, date, sts)
   145	
   146	        v.Set("X-Amz-Signature", signature) // task4
   147	
   148	        // According to the Java source and manual testing, all values in our
   149	        // challenge map must be lowercased, and we MUST have host, and we MUST
   150	        // have version, and version MUST be 2020_10_22.
   151	        keyvals := make(map[string]string)
   152	        for key, values := range v {
   153	                keyvals[strings.ToLower(key)] = values[0]
   154	        }
   155	        keyvals["host"] = host
   156	        keyvals["version"] = "2020_10_22"
   157	        ua := auth.UserAgent
   158	        if ua == "" {
   159	                ua = strings.Join([]string{"franz-go", runtime.Version(), hostname}, "/")
   160	        }
   161	        keyvals["user-agent"] = ua
   162	
   163	        marshaled, err := json.Marshal(keyvals)
   164	        if err != nil {
   165	                return nil, err
   166	        }
   167	        return marshaled, nil
   168	}
   169	
   170	// https://docs.aws.amazon.com/general/latest/gr/sigv4-create-string-to-sign.html
   171	// "CredentialScope", Part 3
   172	func scope(date, region string) string {
   173	        return strings.Join([]string{date, region, service, "aws4_request"}, "/")
   174	}
   175	
   176	// https://docs.aws.amazon.com/general/latest/gr/sigv4-create-canonical-request.html
   177	func task1(host, qps string) []byte {
   178	        // We start with our defined method, "GET", and the defined empty path,
   179	        // "/". For query parameters, we have to escape +'s with %20, but we did
   180	        // that above when building our URL.
   181	        //
   182	        //   HTTPRequestMethod + '\n' +
   183	        //   CanonicalURI + '\n' +
   184	        //   CanonicalQueryString + '\n' +
   185	        canon := make([]byte, 0, 200)
   186	        canon = append(canon, "GET\n"...)
   187	        canon = append(canon, "/\n"...)
   188	        canon = append(canon, qps...)
   189	        canon = append(canon, '\n')
   190	
   191	        // We only sign one header, the host. Each signed header is followed by
   192	        // a newline, and then the canonical header block is followed itself by
   193	        // a newline.
   194	        //
   195	        //   CanonicalHeaders + '\n' +
   196	        //   SignedHeaders + '\n' +
   197	        canon = append(canon, "host:"...)
   198	        canon = append(canon, host...)
   199	        canon = append(canon, "\n\nhost\n"...)
   200	
   201	        // Finally, we add our empty body.
   202	        //
   203	        //   HexEncode(Hash(RequestPayload))
   204	        const emptyBody = "e3b0c44298fc1c149afbf4c8996fb92427ae41e4649b934ca495991b7852b855"
   205	        return append(canon, emptyBody...)
   206	}
   207	
   208	// https://docs.aws.amazon.com/general/latest/gr/sigv4-create-string-to-sign.html
   209	func task2(timestamp, scope string, canonicalRequest []byte) []byte {
   210	        toSign := make([]byte, 0, 512)
   211	        toSign = append(toSign, "AWS4-HMAC-SHA256\n"...)
   212	        toSign = append(toSign, timestamp...)
   213	        toSign = append(toSign, '\n')
   214	        toSign = append(toSign, scope...)
   215	        toSign = append(toSign, '\n')
   216	        canonHash := sha256.Sum256(canonicalRequest)
   217	        hexBuf := make([]byte, 64) // 32 bytes to 64
   218	        hex.Encode(hexBuf, canonHash[:])
   219	        toSign = append(toSign, hexBuf...)
   220	        return toSign

   263	func identifyRegion(host string) (string, error) {
   264	        for _, suffix := range suffixes {
   265	                if strings.HasSuffix(host, suffix) {
   266	                        serviceRegion := strings.TrimSuffix(host, suffix)

        return err
}

func (c *KafkaConsumer) mskIAMMechanism() (sasl.Mechanism, error) {
        if c.config.AssumeRoleARN == "" {
                return mskaws.Auth{
                        AccessKey: c.config.SASLUser,
                        SecretKey: c.config.SASLPassword,
                }.AsManagedStreamingIAMMechanism(), nil
        }

        loadOpts := []func(*config.LoadOptions) error{}
        if c.config.CredentialsProfile != "" {
                loadOpts = append(loadOpts, config.WithSharedConfigProfile(c.config.CredentialsProfile))
        }

        ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 5*time.Second)
        defer cancel()
        awsCfg, err := config.LoadDefaultConfig(ctx, loadOpts...)
        if err != nil {
                return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to load AWS config: %w", err)
        }

        stsClient := sts.NewFromConfig(awsCfg)
        assumeRoleProvider := stscreds.NewAssumeRoleProvider(stsClient, c.config.AssumeRoleARN)
        credentials := awssdk.NewCredentialsCache(assumeRoleProvider)

        return mskaws.ManagedStreamingIAM(func(ctx context.Context) (mskaws.Auth, error) {
                creds, err := credentials.Retrieve(ctx)
                if err != nil {
                        return mskaws.Auth{}, fmt.Errorf("failed to retrieve AWS credentials: %w", err)
                }
                return mskaws.Auth{
                        AccessKey:    creds.AccessKeyID,
                        SecretKey:    creds.SecretAccessKey,
                        SessionToken: creds.SessionToken,
                }, nil
        }), nil
}'

    48	type KafkaConsumer struct {
    49	        name       string
    50	        client     *kgo.Client
    51	        dispatcher Dispatcher
    52	        config     KafkaConfig
    53	        // consumersMu protects the consumers map. During normal operation, concurrent access is already
    54	        // prevented: franz-go serializes assigned/revoked/lost callbacks, and BlockRebalanceOnPoll
    55	        // prevents callbacks from firing while pollUntilFatal reads the map. The mutex is needed
    56	        // for shutdown, when the main goroutine accesses the map (via allTopicPartitions/killConsumers)
    57	        // while the group management goroutine may still be running callbacks. Must not be held
    58	        // during killConsumers' wg.Wait() to avoid blocking concurrent callbacks.
    59	        consumersMu    sync.Mutex
    60	        consumers      map[topicPartition]*partitionConsumer
    61	        doneCh         chan struct{}
    62	        common         *consumerCommon
    63	        testOnlyConfig testOnlyConfig
    64	}
    65	
    66	func NewKafkaConsumer(
    67	        config KafkaConfig, dispatcher Dispatcher, common *consumerCommon,
    68	) (*KafkaConsumer, error) {
    69	        if len(config.Brokers) == 0 {
    70	                return nil, errors.New("brokers required")
    71	        }
    72	        if len(config.Topics) == 0 {
    73	                return nil, errors.New("topics required")
    74	        }
    75	        if len(config.ConsumerGroup) == 0 {
    76	                return nil, errors.New("consumer_group required")
    77	        }
    78	        if config.MaxPollRecords == 0 {
    79	                config.MaxPollRecords = 100
    80	        }
    81	        if config.FetchMaxWait == 0 {
    82	                config.FetchMaxWait = configtypes.Duration(500 * time.Millisecond)
    83	        }
    84	        if config.PartitionQueueMaxSize == -1 {
    85	                config.PartitionQueueMaxSize = 0
    86	        } else if config.PartitionQueueMaxSize == 0 {
    87	                config.PartitionQueueMaxSize = 1000
    88	        }
    89	        consumer := &KafkaConsumer{
    90	                name:       common.name,
    91	                dispatcher: dispatcher,
    92	                config:     config,
    93	                consumers:  make(map[topicPartition]*partitionConsumer),
    94	                doneCh:     make(chan struct{}),
    95	                common:     common,
    96	        }
    97	        cl, err := consumer.initClient()
    98	        if err != nil {
    99	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("error init Kafka client: %w", err)
   100	        }
   101	        consumer.client = cl
   102	        return consumer, nil
   103	}

   107	// kgoZerologAdapter adapts zerolog.Logger to kgo.Logger interface.
   108	type kgoZerologAdapter struct {
   109	        log zerolog.Logger
   110	}
   111	
   112	func (l *kgoZerologAdapter) Level() kgo.LogLevel {
   113	        switch {
   114	        case logging.Enabled(logging.TraceLevel):
   115	                return kgo.LogLevelDebug // Kafka client debug level is more like our trace.
   116	        case logging.Enabled(logging.InfoLevel):
   117	                return kgo.LogLevelInfo
   118	        case logging.Enabled(logging.WarnLevel):
   119	                return kgo.LogLevelWarn
   120	        case logging.Enabled(logging.ErrorLevel):
   121	                return kgo.LogLevelError
   122	        default:
   123	                return kgo.LogLevelNone
   124	        }
   125	}
   126	
   127	func (l *kgoZerologAdapter) Log(level kgo.LogLevel, msg string, keyvals ...any) {
   128	        var e *zerolog.Event
   129	        switch level {
   130	        case kgo.LogLevelError:
   131	                e = l.log.Error()
   132	        case kgo.LogLevelWarn:
   133	                e = l.log.Warn()
   134	        case kgo.LogLevelInfo:
   135	                e = l.log.Info()
   136	        case kgo.LogLevelDebug:
   137	                e = l.log.Trace() // Kafka client debug level is more like our trace.
   138	        default:
   139	                return
   140	        }
   141	        for i := 0; i+1 < len(keyvals); i += 2 {
   142	                if key, ok := keyvals[i].(string); ok {
   143	                        e = e.Interface(key, keyvals[i+1])
   144	                }
   145	        }
   146	        e.Msg(msg)
   147	}

   187	        stsClient := sts.NewFromConfig(awsCfg)
   188	        assumeRoleProvider := stscreds.NewAssumeRoleProvider(stsClient, c.config.AssumeRoleARN)
   189	        credentials := awssdk.NewCredentialsCache(assumeRoleProvider)
   190	
   191	        return mskaws.ManagedStreamingIAM(func(ctx context.Context) (mskaws.Auth, error) {
   192	                creds, err := credentials.Retrieve(ctx)
   193	                if err != nil {
   194	                        return mskaws.Auth{}, fmt.Errorf("failed to retrieve AWS credentials: %w", err)
   195	                }
   196	                return mskaws.Auth{
   197	                        AccessKey:    creds.AccessKeyID,
   198	                        SecretKey:    creds.SecretAccessKey,
   199	                        SessionToken: creds.SessionToken,
   200	                }, nil
   201	        }), nil
   202	}
   203	
   204	func (c *KafkaConsumer) initClient() (*kgo.Client, error) {
   205	        opts := []kgo.Opt{
   206	                kgo.SeedBrokers(c.config.Brokers...),
   207	                kgo.ConsumeTopics(c.config.Topics...),
   208	                kgo.ConsumerGroup(c.config.ConsumerGroup),
   209	                kgo.OnPartitionsAssigned(c.assigned),
   210	                kgo.OnPartitionsRevoked(c.revoked),
   211	                kgo.OnPartitionsLost(c.lost),
   212	                kgo.AutoCommitMarks(),
   213	                kgo.BlockRebalanceOnPoll(),
   214	                kgo.ClientID(kafkaClientID),
   215	                kgo.FetchMaxWait(time.Duration(c.config.FetchMaxWait)),
   216	                kgo.WithLogger(&kgoZerologAdapter{log: c.common.log}),
   217	        }
   218	        if c.config.InstanceID != "" { // Important to keep separate, otherwise pointer to empty string is used in kgo.InstanceID.
   219	                opts = append(opts, kgo.InstanceID(c.config.InstanceID))
   220	        }
   221	        if c.config.FetchMaxBytes > 0 {
   222	                opts = append(opts, kgo.FetchMaxBytes(c.config.FetchMaxBytes))
   223	        }
   224	        if !c.config.FetchReadUncommitted {
   225	                opts = append(opts, kgo.FetchIsolationLevel(kgo.ReadCommitted()))
   226	        } else {
   227	                opts = append(opts, kgo.FetchIsolationLevel(kgo.ReadUncommitted()))
   228	        }
   229	        if c.config.TLS.Enabled {
   230	                tlsConfig, err := c.config.TLS.ToGoTLSConfig("kafka:" + c.name)
   231	                if err != nil {
   232	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("error making TLS configuration: %w", err)
   233	                }
   234	                dialer := &tls.Dialer{
   235	                        NetDialer: &net.Dialer{Timeout: 10 * time.Second},

	// The chain of providers that was used to create this provider
	// These values are for reporting purposes and are not meant to be set up directly
	CredentialSources []aws.CredentialSource
}

// NewAssumeRoleProvider constructs and returns a credentials provider that
// will retrieve credentials by assuming a IAM role using STS.
func NewAssumeRoleProvider(client AssumeRoleAPIClient, roleARN string, optFns ...func(*AssumeRoleOptions)) *AssumeRoleProvider {
	o := AssumeRoleOptions{
		Client:  client,
		RoleARN: roleARN,
	}

	for _, fn := range optFns {
		fn(&o)
	}

	return &AssumeRoleProvider{
		options: o,
	}
}

// Retrieve generates a new set of temporary credentials using STS.
func (p *AssumeRoleProvider) Retrieve(ctx context.Context) (aws.Credentials, error) {
	// Apply defaults where parameters are not set.
	if len(p.options.RoleSessionName) == 0 {
		// Try to work out a role name that will hopefully end up unique.
		p.options.RoleSessionName = fmt.Sprintf("aws-go-sdk-%d", time.Now().UTC().UnixNano())
	}
	if p.options.Duration == 0 {
		// Expire as often as AWS permits.
		p.options.Duration = DefaultDuration
	}
	input := &sts.AssumeRoleInput{
		DurationSeconds:   aws.Int32(int32(p.options.Duration / time.Second)),
		PolicyArns:        p.options.PolicyARNs,
		RoleArn:           aws.String(p.options.RoleARN),
		RoleSessionName:   aws.String(p.options.RoleSessionName),
		ExternalId:        p.options.ExternalID,
		SourceIdentity:    p.options.SourceIdentity,
		Tags:              p.options.Tags,
		TransitiveTagKeys: p.options.TransitiveTagKeys,
	}
	if p.options.Policy != nil {
		input.Policy = p.options.Policy
	}
	if p.options.SerialNumber != nil {
		if p.options.TokenProvider != nil {
			input.SerialNumber = p.options.SerialNumber
			code, err := p.options.TokenProvider()
			if err != nil {
				return aws.Credentials{}, err
			}
			input.TokenCode = aws.String(code)
		} else {
			return aws.Credentials{}, fmt.Errorf("assume role with MFA enabled, but TokenProvider is not set")
		}
	}

	resp, err := p.options.Client.AssumeRole(ctx, input)
	if err != nil {
		return aws.Credentials{Source: ProviderName}, err
	}

	var accountID string
	if resp.AssumedRoleUser != nil {
		accountID = getAccountID(resp.AssumedRoleUser)
	}

	return aws.Credentials{
		AccessKeyID:     *resp.Credentials.AccessKeyId,
		SecretAccessKey: *resp.Credentials.SecretAccessKey,
		SessionToken:    *resp.Credentials.SessionToken,
		Source:          ProviderName,

		CanExpire: true,
		Expires:   *resp.Credentials.Expiration,
		AccountID: accountID,
	}, nil
}

+func (c *KafkaConsumer) mskIAMMechanism() (sasl.Mechanism, error) {
+	if c.config.AssumeRoleARN == "" && c.config.CredentialsProfile == "" {
+		return mskaws.Auth{
+			AccessKey: c.config.SASLUser,
+			SecretKey: c.config.SASLPassword,
+		}.AsManagedStreamingIAMMechanism(), nil
+	}
+
+	loadOpts := []func(*config.LoadOptions) error{}
+	if c.config.CredentialsProfile != "" {
+		loadOpts = append(loadOpts, config.WithSharedConfigProfile(c.config.CredentialsProfile))
+	}
+
+	ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 5*time.Second)
+	defer cancel()
+	awsCfg, err := config.LoadDefaultConfig(ctx, loadOpts...)
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to load AWS config: %w", err)
+	}
+
+	credentials := awsCfg.Credentials
+	if c.config.AssumeRoleARN != "" {
+		stsClient := sts.NewFromConfig(awsCfg)
+		assumeRoleProvider := stscreds.NewAssumeRoleProvider(stsClient, c.config.AssumeRoleARN)
+		credentials = awssdk.NewCredentialsCache(assumeRoleProvider)
+	}
+
+	return mskaws.ManagedStreamingIAM(func(ctx context.Context) (mskaws.Auth, error) {
+		creds, err := credentials.Retrieve(ctx)
+		if err != nil {
+			return mskaws.Auth{}, fmt.Errorf("failed to retrieve AWS credentials: %w", err)
+		}
+		return mskaws.Auth{
+			AccessKey:    creds.AccessKeyID,
+			SecretKey:    creds.SecretAccessKey,
+			SessionToken: creds.SessionToken,
+		}, nil
+	}), nil
+}
+

 	opts := []kgo.Opt{
 		kgo.SeedBrokers(c.config.Brokers...),
@@ -214,10 +259,11 @@ func (c *KafkaConsumer) initClient() (*kgo.Client, error) {

 // NatsBroker configuration.
 type NatsBroker struct {
-	NatsPrefixed `mapstructure:",squash" yaml:",inline"`
-
-	// AllowWildcards allows to enable wildcard subscriptions. By default, wildcard subscriptions
-	// are not allowed. Using wildcard subscriptions can't be combined with join/leave events and presence
-	// because subscriptions do not belong to a concrete channel after with wildcards, while join/leave events
-	// require concrete channel to be published. And presence does not make a lot of sense for wildcard
-	// subscriptions - there could be subscribers which use different mask, but still receive subset of updates.
-	// It's required to use channels without wildcards to for mentioned features to work properly. When
-	// using wildcard subscriptions a special care is needed regarding security - pay additional
-	// attention to a proper permission management.
-	AllowWildcards bool `mapstructure:"allow_wildcards" json:"allow_wildcards" envconfig:"allow_wildcards" yaml:"allow_wildcards" toml:"allow_wildcards"`
-
-	// RawMode allows enabling raw communication with Nats. When on, Centrifugo subscribes to channels
-	// without adding any prefixes to channel name. Proper prefixes must be managed by the application in this
-	// case. Data consumed from Nats is sent directly to subscribers without any processing. When publishing
-	// to Nats Centrifugo does not add any prefixes to channel names also. Centrifugo features like Publication
-	// tags, Publication ClientInfo, join/leave events are not supported in raw mode.
-	RawMode RawModeConfig `mapstructure:"raw_mode" json:"raw_mode" envconfig:"raw_mode" yaml:"raw_mode" toml:"raw_mode"`
+        NatsPrefixed `mapstructure:",squash" yaml:",inline"`
+
+        // AllowWildcards allows to enable wildcard subscriptions. By default, wildcard subscriptions
+        // are not allowed. Using wildcard subscriptions can't be combined with join/leave events and presence
+        // because subscriptions do not belong to a concrete channel after with wildcards, while join/leave events
+        // require concrete channel to be published. And presence does not make a lot of sense for wildcard
+        // subscriptions - there could be subscribers which use different mask, but still receive subset of updates.
+        // It's required to use channels without wildcards to for mentioned features to work properly. When
+        // using wildcard subscriptions a special care is needed regarding security - pay additional
+        // attention to a proper permission management.
+        AllowWildcards bool `mapstructure:"allow_wildcards" json:"allow_wildcards" envconfig:"allow_wildcards" yaml:"allow_wildcards" toml:"allow_wildcards"`
+
+        // RawMode allows enabling raw communication with Nats. When on, Centrifugo subscribes to channels
+        // without adding any prefixes to channel name. Proper prefixes must be managed by the application in this
+        // case. Data consumed from Nats is sent directly to subscribers without any processing. When publishing
+        // to Nats Centrifugo does not add any prefixes to channel names also. Centrifugo features like Publication

+        // For example, you have Centrifugo namespace "chat" and using channel "chat:index", but you want to
+        // use channel "chat.index" in Nats. Then you can define SymbolReplacements map like this: `{":": "."}`.

 type Client struct {
-	// Proxy is a configuration for client connection-wide proxies.
-	Proxy ClientProxyContainer `mapstructure:"proxy" json:"proxy" envconfig:"proxy" toml:"proxy" yaml:"proxy"`
-	// AllowedOrigins is a list of allowed origins for client connections.
-	AllowedOrigins []string `mapstructure:"allowed_origins" json:"allowed_origins" envconfig:"allowed_origins" yaml:"allowed_origins" toml:"allowed_origins"`
-	// Token is a configuration for token generation and verification. When enabled, this configuration
-	// is used for both connection and subscription tokens. See also SubscriptionToken to use a separate
-	// configuration for subscription tokens.
-	Token Token `mapstructure:"token" json:"token" envconfig:"token" yaml:"token" toml:"token"`
-	// SubscriptionToken is a configuration for subscription token generation and verification. When enabled,
-	// Centrifugo will use this configuration for subscription tokens only. Configuration in Token is then only
-	// used for connection tokens.
-	SubscriptionToken SubscriptionToken `mapstructure:"subscription_token" json:"subscription_token" envconfig:"subscription_token" yaml:"subscription_token" toml:"subscription_token"`
-	// AllowAnonymousConnectWithoutToken allows to connect to Centrifugo without a token. In this case connection will
-	// be accepted but client will be anonymous (i.e. will have empty user ID).
-	AllowAnonymousConnectWithoutToken bool `mapstructure:"allow_anonymous_connect_without_token" json:"allow_anonymous_connect_without_token" envconfig:"allow_anonymous_connect_without_token" yaml:"allow_anonymous_connect_without_token" toml:"allow_anonymous_connect_without_token"`
-	// DisallowAnonymousConnectionTokens disallows anonymous connection tokens. When enabled, Centrifugo will not
-	// accept connection tokens with empty user ID.
-	DisallowAnonymousConnectionTokens bool `mapstructure:"disallow_anonymous_connection_tokens" json:"disallow_anonymous_connection_tokens" envconfig:"disallow_anonymous_connection_tokens" yaml:"disallow_anonymous_connection_tokens" toml:"disallow_anonymous_connection_tokens"`
-	// PingPong allows configuring application level ping-pong behavior for client connections.
-	PingPong `mapstructure:",squash" yaml:",inline"`
-	// ExpiredConnectionCloseDelay is a delay before closing connection after it becomes expired.
-	ExpiredCloseDelay Duration `mapstructure:"expired_close_delay" json:"expired_close_delay" envconfig:"expired_close_delay" default:"25s" yaml:"expired_close_delay" toml:"expired_close_delay"`
-	// ExpiredSubCloseDelay is a delay before closing subscription after it becomes expired.
-	ExpiredSubCloseDelay Duration `mapstructure:"expired_sub_close_delay" json:"expired_sub_close_delay" envconfig:"expired_sub_close_delay" default:"25s" yaml:"expired_sub_close_delay" toml:"expired_sub_close_delay"`
-	// StaleConnectionCloseDelay is a delay before closing stale connection (which does not authenticate after connecting).
-	StaleCloseDelay Duration `mapstructure:"stale_close_delay" json:"stale_close_delay" envconfig:"stale_close_delay" default:"10s" yaml:"stale_close_delay" toml:"stale_close_delay"`
-	// ChannelLimit is a maximum number of channels client can subscribe to.
-	ChannelLimit int `mapstructure:"channel_limit" json:"channel_limit" envconfig:"channel_limit" default:"128" yaml:"channel_limit" toml:"channel_limit"`
-	// QueueMaxSize is a maximum size of message queue for client connection in bytes.
-	QueueMaxSize int `mapstructure:"queue_max_size" json:"queue_max_size" envconfig:"queue_max_size" default:"1048576" yaml:"queue_max_size" toml:"queue_max_size"`
-	// PresenceUpdateInterval is a period of time how often to update presence info for subscriptions of connected client.
-	PresenceUpdateInterval Duration `mapstructure:"presence_update_interval" json:"presence_update_interval" envconfig:"presence_update_interval" default:"27s" yaml:"presence_update_interval" toml:"presence_update_interval"`
-	// Concurrency is a maximum number of concurrent operations for client connection. If not set only one operation can be processed at a time.
-	Concurrency int `mapstructure:"concurrency" json:"concurrency" envconfig:"concurrency" yaml:"concurrency" toml:"concurrency"`
-	// ChannelPositionCheckDelay is a delay between channel position checks for client subscriptions.
-	ChannelPositionCheckDelay Duration `mapstructure:"channel_position_check_delay" json:"channel_position_check_delay" envconfig:"channel_position_check_delay" default:"40s" yaml:"channel_position_check_delay" toml:"channel_position_check_delay"`
-	// ChannelPositionMaxTimeLag is a maximum allowed time lag for publications for subscribers with positioning on. When
-	// exceeded we mark connection with insufficient state. By default, not used - i.e. Centrifugo does not take lag into
-	// account for positioning. See pub_sub_time_lag_seconds as a helpful Prometheus metric.
-	ChannelPositionMaxTimeLag Duration `mapstructure:"channel_position_max_time_lag" json:"channel_position_max_time_lag" envconfig:"channel_position_max_time_lag" yaml:"channel_position_max_time_lag" toml:"channel_position_max_time_lag"`
-	// ConnectionLimit is a maximum number of connections Centrifugo node can accept.
-	ConnectionLimit int `mapstructure:"connection_limit" json:"connection_limit" envconfig:"connection_limit" yaml:"connection_limit" toml:"connection_limit"`
-	// UserConnectionLimit is a maximum number of connections Centrifugo node can accept from a single user.
-	UserConnectionLimit int `mapstructure:"user_connection_limit" json:"user_connection_limit" envconfig:"user_connection_limit" yaml:"user_connection_limit" toml:"user_connection_limit"`

-	ConnectionRateLimit int `mapstructure:"connection_rate_limit" json:"connection_rate_limit" envconfig:"connection_rate_limit" yaml:"connection_rate_limit" toml:"connection_rate_limit"`
-	// ConnectIncludeServerTime allows to include server time in connect reply of client protocol.

 func decodeToNamedSlice(value string, target interface{}) error {
-	targetVal := reflect.ValueOf(target)
-	if targetVal.Kind() != reflect.Ptr || targetVal.Elem().Kind() != reflect.Slice {
-		return fmt.Errorf("target must be a pointer to a slice")
-	}
-	targetSlice := targetVal.Elem()
-	elemType := targetSlice.Type().Elem()
-
-	if value == "" {
-		// If the value is empty, leave the slice as it is.
-		return nil
-	}
-	if strings.HasPrefix(value, "[") && strings.HasSuffix(value, "]") {
-		// Unmarshal JSON array into a temporary slice
-		if err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(value), target); err != nil {
-			return fmt.Errorf("failed to unmarshal JSON array: %w", err)
-		}
-	} else {
-		// Parse space-separated values
-		for _, item := range strings.Split(value, " ") {
-			elem := reflect.New(elemType).Elem()
-			if elem.Kind() == reflect.Struct {
-				field := elem.FieldByName("Name")
-				if field.IsValid() && field.Kind() == reflect.String {
-					field.SetString(item)
-				}
-			}
-			targetSlice.Set(reflect.Append(targetSlice, elem))
-		}
-	}
-	return nil
+        targetVal := reflect.ValueOf(target)
+        if targetVal.Kind() != reflect.Ptr || targetVal.Elem().Kind() != reflect.Slice {
+                return fmt.Errorf("target must be a pointer to a slice")
+        }
+        targetSlice := targetVal.Elem()
+        elemType := targetSlice.Type().Elem()
+
+        if value == "" {
+                // If the value is empty, leave the slice as it is.
+                return nil
+        }
+        if strings.HasPrefix(value, "[") && strings.HasSuffix(value, "]") {
+                // Unmarshal JSON array into a temporary slice
+                if err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(value), target); err != nil {
+                        return fmt.Errorf("failed to unmarshal JSON array: %w", err)
+                }
+        } else {
+                // Parse space-separated values
+                for _, item := range strings.Split(value, " ") {
+                        elem := reflect.New(elemType).Elem()
+                        if elem.Kind() == reflect.Struct {
+                                field := elem.FieldByName("Name")
+                                if field.IsValid() && field.Kind() == reflect.String {
+                                        field.SetString(item)
+                                }
+                        }
+                        targetSlice.Set(reflect.Append(targetSlice, elem))
+                }
+        }
+        return nil
 }

 func (d *Consumers) Decode(value string) error {
-	return decodeToNamedSlice(value, d)
+        return decodeToNamedSlice(value, d)
 }

-		return errors.New("no Kafka topics provided")
-	}

-		return errors.New("no Kafka consumer group provided")

-		}

+                return errors.New("durable_consumer_name is required for consumer")

+func (c *KafkaConsumer) mskIAMMechanism() (sasl.Mechanism, error) {
+	if c.config.AssumeRoleARN == "" && c.config.CredentialsProfile == "" {
+		return mskaws.Auth{
+			AccessKey: c.config.SASLUser,
+			SecretKey: c.config.SASLPassword,
+		}.AsManagedStreamingIAMMechanism(), nil
+	}
+
+	loadOpts := []func(*config.LoadOptions) error{}
+	if c.config.CredentialsProfile != "" {
+		loadOpts = append(loadOpts, config.WithSharedConfigProfile(c.config.CredentialsProfile))
+	}
+
+	ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 5*time.Second)
+	defer cancel()
+	awsCfg, err := config.LoadDefaultConfig(ctx, loadOpts...)
+	if err != nil {
+		return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to load AWS config: %w", err)
+	}
+
+	credentials := awsCfg.Credentials
+	if c.config.AssumeRoleARN != "" {
+		stsClient := sts.NewFromConfig(awsCfg)
+		assumeRoleProvider := stscreds.NewAssumeRoleProvider(stsClient, c.config.AssumeRoleARN)
+		credentials = awssdk.NewCredentialsCache(assumeRoleProvider)
+	}
+
+	return mskaws.ManagedStreamingIAM(func(ctx context.Context) (mskaws.Auth, error) {
+		creds, err := credentials.Retrieve(ctx)
+		if err != nil {
+			return mskaws.Auth{}, fmt.Errorf("failed to retrieve AWS credentials: %w", err)
+		}
+		return mskaws.Auth{
+			AccessKey:    creds.AccessKeyID,
+			SecretKey:    creds.SecretAccessKey,
+			SessionToken: creds.SessionToken,
+		}, nil
+	}), nil
+}
+

-	// DisableClosingHandshake disables WebSocket closing handshake. This restores the behavior prior to
-	// Centrifugo v6.5.1 where server never sent a close frame on connection close initiated by server.

 // NatsBroker configuration.
 type NatsBroker struct {
-	NatsPrefixed `mapstructure:",squash" yaml:",inline"`
-
-	// AllowWildcards allows to enable wildcard subscriptions. By default, wildcard subscriptions
-	// are not allowed. Using wildcard subscriptions can't be combined with join/leave events and presence
-	// because subscriptions do not belong to a concrete channel after with wildcards, while join/leave events
-	// require concrete channel to be published. And presence does not make a lot of sense for wildcard
-	// subscriptions - there could be subscribers which use different mask, but still receive subset of updates.
-	// It's required to use channels without wildcards to for mentioned features to work properly. When
-	// using wildcard subscriptions a special care is needed regarding security - pay additional
-	// attention to a proper permission management.
-	AllowWildcards bool `mapstructure:"allow_wildcards" json:"allow_wildcards" envconfig:"allow_wildcards" yaml:"allow_wildcards" toml:"allow_wildcards"`
-
-	// RawMode allows enabling raw communication with Nats. When on, Centrifugo subscribes to channels
-	// without adding any prefixes to channel name. Proper prefixes must be managed by the application in this
-	// case. Data consumed from Nats is sent directly to subscribers without any processing. When publishing
-	// to Nats Centrifugo does not add any prefixes to channel names also. Centrifugo features like Publication
-	// tags, Publication ClientInfo, join/leave events are not supported in raw mode.
-	RawMode RawModeConfig `mapstructure:"raw_mode" json:"raw_mode" envconfig:"raw_mode" yaml:"raw_mode" toml:"raw_mode"`
+        NatsPrefixed `mapstructure:",squash" yaml:",inline"`
+
+        // AllowWildcards allows to enable wildcard subscriptions. By default, wildcard subscriptions
+        // are not allowed. Using wildcard subscriptions can't be combined with join/leave events and presence
+        // because subscriptions do not belong to a concrete channel after with wildcards, while join/leave events
+        // require concrete channel to be published. And presence does not make a lot of sense for wildcard
+        // subscriptions - there could be subscribers which use different mask, but still receive subset of updates.
+        // It's required to use channels without wildcards to for mentioned features to work properly. When
+        // using wildcard subscriptions a special care is needed regarding security - pay additional
+        // attention to a proper permission management.
+        AllowWildcards bool `mapstructure:"allow_wildcards" json:"allow_wildcards" envconfig:"allow_wildcards" yaml:"allow_wildcards" toml:"allow_wildcards"`
+
+        // RawMode allows enabling raw communication with Nats. When on, Centrifugo subscribes to channels
+        // without adding any prefixes to channel name. Proper prefixes must be managed by the application in this
+        // case. Data consumed from Nats is sent directly to subscribers without any processing. When publishing
+        // to Nats Centrifugo does not add any prefixes to channel names also. Centrifugo features like Publication
+        // tags, Publication ClientInfo, join/leave events are not supported in raw mode.

-	// configuration for subscription tokens.
-	Token Token `mapstructure:"token" json:"token" envconfig:"token" yaml:"token" toml:"token"`

-	// Centrifugo will use this configuration for subscription tokens only. Configuration in Token is then only
-	// used for connection tokens.
-	SubscriptionToken SubscriptionToken `mapstructure:"subscription_token" json:"subscription_token" envconfig:"subscription_token" yaml:"subscription_token" toml:"subscription_token"`
-	// AllowAnonymousConnectWithoutToken allows to connect to Centrifugo without a token. In this case connection will
